However, this time the front desk service slapped me hard in the face. After staying for three days (it was supposed to be four days), the result was Wednesday morning. The man on duty at the front desk had a very indifferent attitude, even a bit of a drag. It really made me feel very angry at the timeüò°...I'm not unreasonable at all. Every time I comment on Dorsett, I always rate it very highly. Except today...
Here's what happened: I called the front desk at 10:00 this morning to ask if I could extend my stay in the original room (of course it was my fault that I didn't apply for the extension one day in advance). I thought my inquiry attitude was very good, but the result was the first. Cold water was poured on me, and a man at the front desk responded with a very cold attitude: No, I wanted to ask again if I could change to another room type, but the result was only two words, no, no, without explaining or thinking of a plan. I don‚Äôt have a plan to say sorry to the customer. I don‚Äôt have any of these. I just hung up the phone after saying it three times. It made me feel like I was disturbing him with this call. Is it an express hotel that I am staying in? Maybe the attitude of Express Hotel is better...

After hurriedly packing up my things, the cleaning lady was very nice and told me that someone was checking out and asked me to go to the front desk to ask and give a thumbs up to the housekeeping department üëç

As a result, I went to the front desk and met the male receptionist in person. I thought there were many customers at the front desk, so it was understandable that I was in a hurry when I hung up the phone just now. However, it turned out that it was just me and one customer, and the customer did not ask him to handle the matter, but another young lady. The front desk was doing the processing, and the male receptionist didn't know what he was doing. He said hello and took my card. I boldly asked if there was a room available. He said coldly without raising his head and said no, and left. I stood there, wanting to argue, but forget it... I even said that I would just change to another hotel, and they ignored me...

Next, the concierge was very polite to help me carry my luggage and send me to the car, which was greatüëç. Also, the lady who called me to ask about my request in advance before check-in also liked itüëç

So this time I praise the housekeeping department and the concierge department, but I am disappointed at the front desk. It was only the male front desk on Wednesday morning, which is a bit behind the service level of Dorsett...

Not to mention, now I am looking for a hotel in the rain with my luggage in messy condition. I hope that the next hotel will make me happier today!

msg:The hotel that my colleague helped to book is probably for the five-star hotel and the food praised in the evaluation. Although I have doubts about the fact that five-star hotels do not have swimming pools, it is hard to accept the city center + food.
When we got off the car on the side of the road in front of the hotel, the shape of the building, the door, and the hawkers in the surrounding mobile stalls, my intuition is at most 4 stars. Walking into the lobby, building materials were being disassembled inside. All kinds of noise and the hustle and bustle of the front desk affected my senses. The rating dropped directly to three stars. At that time, I had the idea of changing hotels. Unfortunately, Chengdu is holding a sugar, tobacco and alcohol exhibition during this period, not only the prices have skyrocketed, but it is even more difficult to find vacant rooms. You can only look forward to the legendary food.
The next day‚Äôs breakfast was temporarily set on the sixth floor for some reason. It was a simple 3-star restaurant. In the next few days, it was restored to the restaurant on the 2nd floor. The variety increased a little, at most 4-star standard. I can‚Äôt see the local characteristics, and it‚Äôs frozen and ready-made Most of them, especially the frozen fried dough sticks, were so stiff and ugly that I even wondered if I had come to Chengdu, a gourmet paradise. Maybe the friends who gave good reviews have different perceptions of food, but as a person who travels all year round, was born in Chengdu and has been to Chengdu several times, this by no means represents the level of Chengdu. The hotel is just beside the road, there is Line 1 20 meters away, it is convenient to travel, and it is about 2 kilometers to Kuanzhai Alley. Objectively speaking, the hotel's rooms are good, with reasonable layout, spacious and clean, and no peculiar smell.
In addition, talk about an incident encountered in the hotel. On the second night of my stay, at around 23:00, I lay on the bed in a daze and was about to fall asleep. The door of the room was suddenly opened, and two men‚Äôs loud voices and exclamations woke me up...... My explanation is that the intern made a mistake, the guest went to the wrong room, and the hotel waived the breakfast fee as compensation. I have no intention of blaming the interns, and I don't want the hotel to punish the interns excessively. What I don't understand is: During the check-in process, did the person who instructs the interns carefully confirm? Also, how can the key cards in other rooms open my room? Is there a problem with the hotel computer system? Furthermore, for business travelers, the free breakfast fee has no real comfort value, not to mention that breakfast is unattractive.
To sum up, from the hotel's hardware facilities, catering standards, service quality, and emergency methods, no matter from which angle, I would like to ask how this five-star rating was obtained.

Surroundings: Subway stations, convenience stores and hot pot restaurants are right in front of the hotel, and the distance is no more than 30 meters. Others: There is also a Starbucks coffee service (not a shop) on the first floor, but unfortunately I didn't have time to try it. In addition, there is a coffee shop, but it is supposed to be tea tasting, and there are young ladies who can play music (guzheng), which is very comfortable.

Summary: After commenting on some health details, I haven't found too many problems in general, but some blind spots and inconspicuous places are really not in place. In fact, the hotel is very cost-effective, it is worth considering staying.
